<Name>Ryant Takai</Name>< review>
This place rocks! D-lishousness all up & down the menu.  I have been to many Chinese restaurants throughout Southern California and this hole in the wall is one of a kind.     I have been here with my fiancee & our little one of 7 years.      So far we have sampled their Crispy noodle Chow mein *all styles*,  Fried rice *all styles*, Wonton noodle soups *roasted duck/BBQ-pork*, Chinese broccoli with garlic, Bok-choi with garlic, Mao po tofu,  Fried Chicken *appetizers* Egg Rolls,  Salt & Spicy Jumbo Shrimp *tapioca battered* (a must try),
Roasted Duck, BBQ-pork, General Tsao's Chicken.
It gets busy and packed all the time so arrive early with a big appetite. They have excellent service and will accommodate your every salivatory needs.
We will be back for the rest of the menu, til then I am most sure whatever you decide to sample, you won't be disappointed.
Enjoy!</review>

I've been eating at A1 for many years.  Have always enjoyed the food.  This evening my family of 5 came for dinner to celebrate my birthday January 29, 2020 at 5pm.   My mother arrived with my brother first, the older Chinese lady whom I've not seen here before didn't say one word to my mom or brother, she was obviously in a bad mood.

The charge made on my card reverted to $4 after it was closed out. If you use a card, it puts a hold of $13 on it. It's insane they do that, but I wish they had signs at the machine stating this.

<Name>Valerie Zelinka< /Name><date>1588218723823<//date><rate>5< /rate>< text>
I returned from a trip up north and my car was FILTHY; my front window was full of bug guts.  All the regular car wash places were closed due to COVID-19, so, I had to use a coin-operated car wash and wash the car myself.  I researched reviews and found this place.  I had never been here before so I had to study all of the wash cycles and amenities available.  One no-no is to use your own bucket; they have adequate signs with rules posted.  I used all wash/rinse/and protective coating cycles available: a total of 8.  Each cycle cost $2 for 4 minutes.  I have a mid-sized/4-door sedan style car and 4 minutes was enough time.  I did bring my own mitt/sham for extra cleaning and rubbing in the suds.  I thought there was a lot of suds and that the brushes worked very well.; the water pressure was excellent and the facility itself is kept very clean. The hot air blower helped tremendously to get rid of the large water spots and helped me to dry the car faster overall; I only used one towel to dry the entire car.  I was in the stall for a good 30 minutes with no pressure to hurry up and move along.  After I completed the final rinse, I pulled forward to wipe down the car and wash my windows. The wash brushes available cleaned up the bug guts on the front window and front bumper.  There is a vacuum but I did not use it; other people were using them and I could tell that the vacuums had a lot of power.  I am not sure how much they cost.   My car was sooo clean afterwards and I was very satisfied.  I will use this car wash again.  Finally, they take quarters and credit cards and there is a change machine on site.  I counted 8 stalls.</text>

<review>(Translated by Google) This place is both a cafe and a bar. Sometimes they have programs like karaoke and comedy at this shop. When I go in the morning and the shop has just opened, the owner of the shop is friendly and polite, and they tell me that every time it opens at 8:30 in the morning, but when I arrive, it is less than 8 o'clock. However, the owner also made the coffee I ordered. The price is a bit expensive and the taste is not much better than other places. Most importantly, the service atmosphere is friendly and feels like a coffee shop in the village, which is different from us drinking Starbucks coffee.

< Text>
Decided to try this new place. Not really authentic Pupusas. They are more like Salvadorean Pupusas with Mexican ingredients. They use pinto beans instead of black beans, the cheese they use isn't good quality cheese, and there ingredients proportion is off. I ordered revueltas and I might have well has gotten a bean and cheese because there was no chicharron in mine. Tasted like they used canned beans and not fresh ones. The best thing I liked was the Jamaica drink. Also, when we asked for Salvadorean Horchata, they only had Mexican Horchata which only confirmed they are not authentic.. The chips and Salsa were okay but the salsa tasted like it was also from a can and I could tell it was going bad. The curtido was additionally not good, needed more oregano and you can tell they used canned pickled jalapenos.<//Text>

<rating>5<//rating>< Review>
First visit, will have to come back at least 2 more times. Overall score 4.4, but due to unusual circumstance deserved 5 stars.
Let me explain, Covina has some real gems when it comes to Mexican food, and this unassuming shop is one. It is hidden, good luck seeing it from the street. Parking isn't good, COVID tent doesn't help, will be better when restrictions end. (County CDC guidelines are posted very visibly, excellent job there).  It is not an easy location to get to heading north or west. No bathrooms that I saw. Parking, counter, seating are all accessible.
As for the food, outstanding. Do not take a date here as your first stop, when the date is nearly over and you're both hungry cause it went really well and you didn't eat anything cause you were too nervous, then come here for food, trust me your date will love it. If the date didn't go well, drop them off and come here by yourself, at least you will get some good food at a good price. Staff are phenomenal, beyond helpful, if the food wasn't great would still come back at least one more time. Food was prepared quickly and exceeded my expectations. The breakfast burrito was good, as were the asada and carnitas tacos. Breakfast burrito uses fries which are fine, but combo that with the fries for asada fries, you will have something amazing. Tried the chile verde too, was very good, could have used a slightly stronger kick with the chile, but just add some green sauce. The tacos were a little oily, but not in a bad way, breakfast burrito was not oily at all. Beans were good. Will return for a Chile Verde, Colorado, and a Steak Picado burrito in the future. Also need to try the rice. Looking forward to next visit. Highly recommend obviously.< /Review>
